  - **Relay state transition examples (policy):**
    - **DIRECTIVE reset:** State with `architect_chat_id=warm-arch`, `developer_chat_id=warm-dev` → process `DIRECTIVE` → both cleared before `_dispatch_developer`; first spawn receives `chat_id=""` (full `DEVELOPER_PROMPT`).
    - **NACK warm retry:** After first successful developer spawn (`developer_chat_id` set), `NACK` with `next_actor=developer` → next spawn reuses same `chat_id`, short `(Relay: …)` prompt only.
    - **Strike-3 escalation:** After DIRECTIVE + three `NACK` lines, third retry uses escalation model and `chat_id=""` for developer spawn; state stores new developer id after spawn.
    - **Strike-4 operator:** Fourth `NACK` appends `Operator` INFO, no further developer dispatch (`spawn` count stays at DIRECTIVE + 3 NACK spawns = 4 total when DIRECTIVE precedes the NACK chain).
